Benchmarks for decomposition¶

RandomizedPCA-arcene-fit_unsup¶

Benchmark setup

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('arcene')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)

Benchmark statement

obj.fit(X)

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('arcene')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)
obj.fit(X)

   332                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   333                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   334
   335                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   336                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   337
   338                                                   Parameters
   339                                                   ----------
   340                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   341                                                       Training set.
   342
   343                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   344                                                       Target values.
   345
   346                                                   Returns
   347                                                   -------
   348                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   349                                                       Transformed array.
   350
   351                                                   Notes
   352                                                   -----
   353                                                   This method just calls fit and transform consecutively, i.e., it is not
   354                                                   an optimized implementation of fit_transform, unlike other transformers
   355                                                   such as PCA.
   356
   357                                                   """
   358         1            5      5.0      0.0          if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360         1      3061106 3061106.0    100.0              return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   332                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   333                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   334
   335                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   336                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   337
   338                                                   Parameters
   339                                                   ----------
   340                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   341                                                       Training set.
   342
   343                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   344                                                       Target values.
   345
   346                                                   Returns
   347                                                   -------
   348                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   349                                                       Transformed array.
   350
   351                                                   Notes
   352                                                   -----
   353                                                   This method just calls fit and transform consecutively, i.e., it is not
   354                                                   an optimized implementation of fit_transform, unlike other transformers
   355                                                   such as PCA.
   356
   357                                                   """
   358         1            5      5.0      0.0          if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360         1      1173511 1173511.0    100.0              return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   307                                               def fit(self, X, y=None, homoscedastic=True):
   308                                                   """Additionally to PCA.fit, learns a covariance model
   309
   310                                                   Parameters
   311                                                   ----------
   312                                                   X : array of shape(n_samples, n_dim)
   313                                                       The data to fit
   314
   315                                                   homoscedastic : bool, optional,
   316                                                       If True, average variance across remaining dimensions
   317                                                   """
   318         1         7052   7052.0      8.0          PCA.fit(self, X)
   319         1            7      7.0      0.0          self.dim = X.shape[1]
   320         1          129    129.0      0.1          Xr = X - self.mean_
   321         1         1039   1039.0      1.2          Xr -= np.dot(np.dot(Xr, self.components_.T), self.components_)
   322         1            6      6.0      0.0          n_samples = X.shape[0]
   323         1            4      4.0      0.0          if self.dim <= self.n_components:
   324                                                       delta = np.zeros(self.dim)
   325         1            3      3.0      0.0          elif homoscedastic:
   326                                                       delta = (Xr ** 2).sum() * np.ones(self.dim) \
   327         1          170    170.0      0.2                      / (n_samples * self.dim)
   328                                                   else:

   334         1            4      4.0      0.0          return self

   196                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   197                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   198
   199                                                   Parameters
   200                                                   ----------
   201                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   202                                                       Training data, where n_samples in the number of samples
   203                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   204
   205                                                   Returns
   206                                                   -------
   207                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   208
   209                                                   """
   210         1         7010   7010.0     99.4          U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   211         1            9      9.0      0.1          U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   212
   213         1            3      3.0      0.0          if self.whiten:
   214                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   215                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   216                                                   else:
   217                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   218         1           28     28.0      0.4              U *= S[:self.n_components]
   219
   220         1            3      3.0      0.0          return U

   197                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   198
   199                                                   Parameters
   200                                                   ----------
   201                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   202                                                       Training data, where n_samples in the number of samples
   203                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   204
   205                                                   Returns
   206                                                   -------
   207                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   208
   209                                                   """
   210         1        10776  10776.0     99.4          U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   211         1            9      9.0      0.1          U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   212
   213         1            3      3.0      0.0          if self.whiten:
   214                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   215                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   216                                                   else:
   217                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   218         1           51     51.0      0.5              U *= S[:self.n_components]
   219
   220         1            4      4.0      0.0          return U

Function: fit_transform at line 432

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents
==============================================================
   432                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None):
   433                                                   """Learn a NMF model for the data X and returns the transformed data.
   434
   435                                                   This is more efficient than calling fit followed by transform.
   436
   437                                                   Parameters
   438                                                   ----------
   439
   440                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   441                                                       Data matrix to be decomposed
   442
   443                                                   Returns
   444                                                   -------
   445                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   446                                                       Transformed data
   447                                                   """
   448         1          166    166.0      0.0          X = atleast2d_or_csr(X)
   449         1          181    181.0      0.0          check_non_negative(X, "NMF.fit")
   450
   451         1            6      6.0      0.0          n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   452
   453         1            5      5.0      0.0          if not self.n_components:
   454                                                       self.n_components = n_features
   455
   456         1         4829   4829.0      0.3          W, H = self._init(X)
   457
   458         1           47     47.0      0.0          gradW = (np.dot(W, np.dot(H, H.T))
   459         1          189    189.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(X, H.T, dense_output=True))
   460         1           23     23.0      0.0          gradH = (np.dot(np.dot(W.T, W), H)
   461         1          154    154.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(W.T, X, dense_output=True))
   462         1          306    306.0      0.0          init_grad = norm(np.r_[gradW, gradH.T])
   463         1           16     16.0      0.0          tolW = max(0.001, self.tol) * init_grad  # why max?
   464         1            5      5.0      0.0          tolH = tolW
   465
   466       201         1096      5.5      0.1          for n_iter in xrange(1, self.max_iter + 1):
   467                                                       # stopping condition
   468                                                       # as discussed in paper
   469       200        26558    132.8      1.6              proj_norm = norm(np.r_[gradW[np.logical_or(gradW < 0, W > 0)],
   470       200        65517    327.6      4.0                                     gradH[np.logical_or(gradH < 0, H > 0)]])
   471       200         2927     14.6      0.2              if proj_norm < self.tol * init_grad:
   472                                                           break
   473
   474                                                       # update W
   475       200       844663   4223.3     52.0              W, gradW, iterW = self._update_W(X, H, W, tolW)
   476
   477       200         1668      8.3      0.1              W = W.T
   478       200         1248      6.2      0.1              gradW = gradW.T
   479       200         1005      5.0      0.1              if iterW == 1:
   480         1           10     10.0      0.0                  tolW = 0.1 * tolW
   481
   482                                                       # update H
   483       200       531312   2656.6     32.7              H, gradH, iterH = self._update_H(X, H, W, tolH)
   484
   485       200         1284      6.4      0.1              if iterH == 1:
   486         1           11     11.0      0.0                  tolH = 0.1 * tolH
   487
   488       200        19584     97.9      1.2              self.comp_sparseness_ = _sparseness(H.ravel())
   489       200        21552    107.8      1.3              self.data_sparseness_ = _sparseness(W.ravel())
   490
   491       200         5779     28.9      0.4              if not sp.issparse(X):
   492       200        92177    460.9      5.7                  self.reconstruction_err_ = norm(X - np.dot(W, H))
   493
   494       200         1475      7.4      0.1              self.components_ = H
   495
   496         1            6      6.0      0.0          if n_iter == self.max_iter:
   497         1           18     18.0      0.0              warnings.warn("Iteration limit reached during fit")
   498
   499         1            9      9.0      0.0          return W

   727
   728                                                   Returns
   729                                                   -------
   730                                                   X_new : array, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   731                                                       Transformed data
   732
   733                                                   """
   734                                                   # XXX : kwargs is not documented
   735         1           41     41.0      0.0          X = array2d(X)
   736         1           10     10.0      0.0          n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   737
   738         1            4      4.0      0.0          code = sparse_encode(
   739         1            4      4.0      0.0              X, self.components_, algorithm=self.transform_algorithm,
   740         1            6      6.0      0.0              n_nonzero_coefs=self.transform_n_nonzero_coefs,
   741         1       383151 383151.0    100.0              alpha=self.transform_alpha, n_jobs=self.n_jobs)
   742
   743         1            6      6.0      0.0          if self.split_sign:
   744                                                       # feature vector is split into a positive and negative side
   745                                                       n_samples, n_features = code.shape
   746                                                       split_code = np.empty((n_samples, 2 * n_features))
   747                                                       split_code[:, :n_features] = np.maximum(code, 0)
   748                                                       split_code[:, n_features:] = -np.minimum(code, 0)
   749                                                       code = split_code
   750
   751         1            3      3.0      0.0          return code

   123                                               def transform(self, X, ridge_alpha=None):
   124                                                   """Least Squares projection of the data onto the sparse components.
   125
   126                                                   To avoid instability issues in case the system is under-determined,
   127                                                   regularization can be applied (Ridge regression) via the
   128                                                   `ridge_alpha` parameter.
   129
   130                                                   Note that Sparse PCA components orthogonality is not enforced as in PCA
   131                                                   hence one cannot use a simple linear projection.
   132
   133                                                   Parameters
   134                                                   ----------
   135                                                   X: array of shape (n_samples, n_features)
   136                                                       Test data to be transformed, must have the same number of
   137                                                       features as the data used to train the model.
   138
   139                                                   ridge_alpha: float, default: 0.01
   140                                                       Amount of ridge shrinkage to apply in order to improve
   141                                                       conditioning.
   142
   143                                                   Returns
   144                                                   -------
   145                                                   X_new array, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   146                                                       Transformed data.
   147                                                   """
   148         1            6      6.0      0.9          ridge_alpha = self.ridge_alpha if ridge_alpha is None else ridge_alpha
   149         1            7      7.0      1.1          U = ridge_regression(self.components_.T, X.T, ridge_alpha,
   150         1          505    505.0     79.7                               solver='dense_cholesky')
   151         1           44     44.0      6.9          s = np.sqrt((U ** 2).sum(axis=0))
   152         1           27     27.0      4.3          s[s == 0] = 1
   153         1           42     42.0      6.6          U /= s
   154         1            3      3.0      0.5          return U

   332                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   333                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   334
   335                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   336                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   337
   338                                                   Parameters
   339                                                   ----------
   340                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   341                                                       Training set.
   342
   343                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   344                                                       Target values.
   345
   346                                                   Returns
   347                                                   -------
   348                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   349                                                       Transformed array.
   350
   351                                                   Notes
   352                                                   -----
   353                                                   This method just calls fit and transform consecutively, i.e., it is not
   354                                                   an optimized implementation of fit_transform, unlike other transformers
   355                                                   such as PCA.
   356
   357                                                   """
   358         1            5      5.0      0.0          if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)

   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
